msg:Since I had to take the high-speed train the next morning, I chose a hotel with a high score and not too far from the train station. But overall it was a rather disappointing choice for me.
The lobby is nice and grand as you enter, and there are many other shops. The building where the hotel is located is a complex. In addition to the hotel, there are also other companies.
It's my fault that I didn't see the elevator sign clearly, but the front desk didn't remind me that I got on the wrong elevator. I was very embarrassed and it took me ten minutes to get to my floor. Because there was a prompt to swipe the card in the elevator, I always thought it was the wrong way to swipe the card or the location was wrong. I kept trying, but ended up being transported to another floor. You can only go back to the first floor again. After carefully reading the words above the elevator, I got on the right elevator.
The light in the corridor where the room is located is relatively dark. The door swipe card is also designed in a strange way, it is not on the door, but on the wall. Maybe the designer wanted to be unique, but ended up making another mistake.
The room facilities are very poorly maintained. The toilet has serious cracks and is still in use. The hair dryer is missing a button and you can see that the electrical components inside are still in service. Is there any safety hazard? The bar countertop was stained. Is this the standard for a room costing more than 500 yuan?
The front desk can accept invoice information and can print invoices in advance. But the bank receipt must be given after the ward inspection.
All in all I will definitely not choose this hotel again.
